add_namespace = mod_events.generic_events
add_namespace = mod_events.timed_events

###########################
# Generic Events
###########################

# Army Threat for democratic countries; Civil war
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.generic_events.1
	title = mod_events.generic_events.1.t
	desc = mod_events.generic_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_army
		
	trigger = {
		has_civil_war = no
		has_government = democratic
		fascism > 0.30
		has_stability < 0.15
		threat > 0.10 # checks for world tension
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100 # base mean time 1(100%)/days
		modifier = { # 100% less likely if at war
			factor = 2.00
			has_war = yes
		}
    }
	option = { # Cool down the situation
		name = mod_events.generic_events.1.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }
		add_war_support = -0.10
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
	}
	option = { # Start civil war
		name = mod_events.generic_events.1.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_war_support = 0.20
		add_political_power = 150
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		hidden_effect = { # not shown in tooltip
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -1.00
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = fascism
			size = party_popularity@fascism # this will make the size equal to the popularity of fascism
		}			
	}
	option = { # Give up
		name = mod_events.generic_events.1.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		add_stability = -0.10
		set_politics = {
            ruling_party = fascism
            elections_allowed = no
        }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.10
		}
	}
}
# Workers strike communism uprising; Civil war
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.generic_events.2
	title = mod_events.generic_events.2.t
	desc = mod_events.generic_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_worker_protests
	
	trigger = {
		has_civil_war = no
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
		communism > 0.30
		has_stability < 0.15
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100 # base mean time 1(100%)/days
		modifier = { # 100% less likely if at war
			factor = 2
			has_war = yes
		}
    }
	option = { # Cool down the situation
		name = mod_events.generic_events.2.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		add_war_support = -0.10
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
	}
	option = { # Start civil war
		name = mod_events.generic_events.2.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_political_power = 100
		hidden_effect = {
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -1.00
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = communism
			size = 0.40
		}
	}
	option = { # Give up
		name = mod_events.generic_events.2.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.30
		}
		set_politics = {
            ruling_party = communism
            elections_allowed = no
        }
	}
}
# Freedom shall return, democrats take over; Civil war
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.generic_events.3
	title = mod_events.generic_events.3.t
	desc = mod_events.generic_events.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_democratic_parlament
	
	trigger = {
		has_civil_war = no
		has_war = yes
		NOT = { has_government = democratic }
		democratic > 0.05
		has_war_support < party_popularity@democratic # this will make the size equal to the popularity of democracy
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100 # base mean time 1(100%)/days
		modifier = { # 100% less likely if at war
			factor = 2.00 # multiplication
			has_war = yes
		}
    }
	option = { # Start civil war
		name = mod_events.generic_events.3.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_political_power = 100
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -1.00
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = democratic
			size = 0.40
		}
	}
	option = { # Give up
		name = mod_events.generic_events.3.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.30
		}
		set_politics = {
            ruling_party = democratic
            elections_allowed = yes
        }
	}
}

# Communist strikes; damage to buildings
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.generic_events.5
	title = mod_events.generic_events.5.t
	desc = mod_events.generic_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_FIN_helsinki_bombed
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
		communism > 0.10
		has_stability < 0.40
		threat > 0.10
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20 # base mean time 1(100%)/days
    }
	
	option = { # OK 
		name = mod_events.generic_events.5.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_manpower = -200
		random_list = {
			33 = {
				THIS = {
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						damage_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							damage = 2.00
						}
					}
				}
			} 33 = {
				THIS = {
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						damage_building = {
							type = infrastructure
							damage = 2.00
						}
					}
				}
			} 33 = {
				THIS = {
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						damage_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							damage = 2.00
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.005
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # By force
		name = mod_events.generic_events.5.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		add_manpower = -5000
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.02
		}
	}
}

# Chamberlain is back
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.generic_events.6
	title = mod_events.generic_events.6.t
	desc = mod_events.generic_events.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chamberlain
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		has_government = democratic
		has_war_with = GER
		date > 1942.9.11
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
    }
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.generic_events.6.a
		add_political_power = 100
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
        	name = "Chamberlain The Immortal"
        	desc = "POLITICS_NEVILLE_CHAMBERLAIN_DESC"
			picture = GFX_portrait_ENG_neville_chamberlain_immortal
        	expire = "1965.1.1"
        	ideology = conservatism
			traits = { rearmer war_industrialist dictator legitimate_heir }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = mod_events.news.1 days = 2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.generic_events.6.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.2 days = 2 }
	}
}

# 1 # Communism spreads
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.1
	title = mod_events.timed_events.1.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_propaganda
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.10
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_country = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.10
				}
			}
		}
		name = mod_events.timed_events.1.a
	}
}

# 2 # Zombie Outbreak
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.2
	title = mod_events.timed_events.2.t
	
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_state = {
				limit = { is_island_state = no state_population_k > 1000 NOT = { is_controlled_by = ZZZ } } # At least 1 million
				transfer_state_to = ZZZ # Sets ZZZ owner of the state
				add_core_of = ZZZ
				ZZZ = {
					load_oob = "ZZZ_1936" # Get Brainzz Horde template
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Brainzz Horde\" division_template = \"Brainzz Horde\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					count = 10
					owner = ZZZ
				}
			}
			
			ZZZ = { 
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 150 # Since Zombies require 1 piece of equipment to deploy a division
					producer = CHI
				}
			}
		}
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.3 days = 2 }
	}
}
# 3 # God's Plan; The Holy Realm
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.3
	title = mod_events.timed_events.3.t
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { OR = { BHU = { is_ai = no } TIB = { is_ai = no } NEP = { is_ai = no } } } 
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.4 days = 1 }
		} else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = BHU tag = TIB tag = NEP } }
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.4 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.4
	title = mod_events.timed_events.4.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_lhasa
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.4.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = THR
			add_ideas = THR_gods_plan
			create_faction = gods_plan
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
				election_frequency = 48
				long_name = "God's Plan"
				name = "God's Plan"
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 1.00
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "God"
				picture = GFX_portrait_THR_godly_figure
				ideology = despotism
			}
			news_event = { id = mod_events.news.9 days = 3 }
		}
		BHU = {
			if = { limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.5 days = 3 }
				every_core_state = {
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		NEP = {
			if = { limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.5 days = 1 }
				every_core_state = {
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		TIB = {
			if = { limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.5 days = 2 }
				every_core_state = {
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.4.b
		add_stability = -0.10
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.5
	title = mod_events.timed_events.5.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_lhasa
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.5.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		FROM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.5.b
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_war_support = 0.10
		FROM = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
	}
}
# 4 # Random war
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.6
	title = mod_events.timed_events.6.t
	
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_war = no }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { always = yes }
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 6 # Independence wave
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.8
	title = mod_events.timed_events.8.t
	
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clear_array = global.indp_countries
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = { exists = no any_state = { is_core_of = PREV } NOT = { OR = { tag = UKR tag = BEL } } }
			random_select_amount = 3
			add_to_array = { global.indp_countries = THIS }
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.indp_countries
			random_country = {
				limit = { any_controlled_state = { is_core_of = PREV.PREV } }
				release = PREV
				set_truce = {
					target = PREV
					days = 180
				}
				PREV = { # So that the country doesn't lose cores 
					every_owned_state = {
						add_core_of = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { global.indp_country_1 = global.indp_countries^0 }
		set_variable = { global.indp_country_2 = global.indp_countries^1 }
		set_variable = { global.indp_country_3 = global.indp_countries^2 }
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.6 days = 2 }
	}
}
# 7 # Random expansion
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.9
	title = mod_events.timed_events.9.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = { all_owned_state = { is_island_state = no } }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.10 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.10
	title = mod_events.timed_events.10.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_army_training
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_variable = num_neighbors
			clear_array = selected_neighbors
			every_neighbor_country = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ROOT.selected_neighbors = THIS.id } } }
				random_select_amount = 4
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.num_neighbors = 1 }
				add_to_array = { ROOT.selected_neighbors = THIS.id }
			}
			log = "Number of neighbors [ROOT.GetName] has: [?num_neighbors|.0]"
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.10.a
		add_war_support = 0.10
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				var:selected_neighbors^0 = {
					is_major = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				var:selected_neighbors^0 = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				var:selected_neighbors^0 = { num_divisions < ROOT.num_divisions }
			}
		}
		var:selected_neighbors^0 = {
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.10.b
		add_war_support = 0.10
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				var:selected_neighbors^1 = {
					is_major = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				var:selected_neighbors^1 = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				var:selected_neighbors^1 = { num_divisions < ROOT.num_divisions }
			}
		}
		var:selected_neighbors^1 = {
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { num_neighbors > 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.10.c
		add_war_support = 0.10
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				var:selected_neighbors^2 = {
					is_major = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				var:selected_neighbors^2 = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				var:selected_neighbors^2 = { num_divisions < ROOT.num_divisions }
			}
		}
		var:selected_neighbors^2 = {
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { num_neighbors > 2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.10.e
		add_war_support = 0.10
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				var:selected_neighbors^3 = {
					is_major = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				var:selected_neighbors^3 = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				var:selected_neighbors^3 = { num_divisions < ROOT.num_divisions }
			}
		}
		var:selected_neighbors^3 = {
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { num_neighbors > 3 }
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

# 10 # War spirit or peace spirit
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.14
	title = mod_events.timed_events.14.t
	
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.16
	title = mod_events.timed_events.16.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_machine_gunners
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.16.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				FROM = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { FROM = { has_government = fascism } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		} else_if = { limit = { FROM = { has_government = democratic } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		} else_if = { limit = { FROM = { has_government = neutrality } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		} else_if = { limit = { FROM = { has_government = communism } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.20
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
		add_political_power = 100
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_political_power = 25
				add_stability = 0.02
				add_war_support = 0.02
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.18 days = 1 }
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = small_increase
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.16.b
		add_stability = 0.05
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_political_power = -10
				add_stability = -0.02
				add_war_support = -0.02
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.19 days = 1 } }
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = unstable_alliance
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				FROM = { is_enemy_ideology = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				FROM = { num_of_factories < ROOT.num_of_factories }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				ROOT = { is_major = yes }
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = mod_events.timed_events.20.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_other_country = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
			random_other_country = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
				random_other_country = {
					create_faction = anti_player_pact
					add_to_faction = PREV.PREV
					add_to_faction = PREV
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ROOT
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.21 days = 1 }
	}
}

# 12 # Africa
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.22
	title = mod_events.timed_events.22.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { ROOT = { is_ai = no capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa } } }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.23 days = 1 }
		} else = { 
			random_country = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa } }
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.23 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.23
	title = mod_events.timed_events.23.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_african_unity
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		name = mod_events.timed_events.23.a
		set_cosmetic_tag = AFR
		add_ideas = AFR_african_ambission
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
			election_frequency = 48
			long_name = "Absolute Monarchy of King of Africa"
			name = "African Dynasty"
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 1.00
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
        	name = "King of Africa"
			picture = GFX_portrait_AFR_king_of_africa
        	expire = "1965.1.1"
        	ideology = despotism
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		division_template = {
			name = "African Tribal Division"
			regiments = { 
				irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 3 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
				irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 3 }
			}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"African Tribes\" division_template = \"African Tribal Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				count = 10
				owner = ROOT
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { any_owned_state = { is_on_continent = africa } }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.24 days = 1 }
		}
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.10 days = 4 }
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		name = mod_events.timed_events.23.b
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.27
	title = mod_events.timed_events.27.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.28 days = 1 } } # Earthquake
				10 = { if = { limit = { any_owned_state = { is_coastal = yes } } 
						country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.29 days = 1 } # Flood
					} else = {
						country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.28 days = 1 }
					}
				}
				10 = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.30 days = 1 } } # Tornado
				10 = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.31 days = 1 } } # Wildfire
				10 = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.32 days = 1 } } # Lightning Storm
				10 = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.33 days = 1 } } # Hurricane
			}
		}
	}
}

						damage = 1.00

						type = infrastructure
						damage = 1.00
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

		effect_tooltip = {

				damage_building = {

					type = industrial_complex

		}

	}

					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }

			}
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV impassable = no }

					division = "name = \"Random Events Division\" division_template = \"Infantry Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.42 days = 1 }
		}
	}

# 26 # Move industry to desert
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.58
	title = mod_events.timed_events.58.t

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { any_owned_state = { is_desert_state = yes } }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.59 days = 1 }
		} else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = { num_of_factories > 50 any_owned_state = { is_desert_state = yes } }
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.59 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.59
	title = mod_events.timed_events.59.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.59.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_desert
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = mod_events.timed_events.59.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = { limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT is_desert_state = yes }
				add_to_temp_array = { owned_desert_states = THIS }
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = owned_desert_states
				value = v
				add_to_temp_variable = { num_of_owned_desert_states = 1 } # Distribute factories evenly throughout states.
				log = "[ROOT.GetName] owns desert state: [?v.GetID], [?v.GetName]"
			}
			set_temp_variable = { num_of_military_factories_to_desert = num_of_military_factories }
			set_temp_variable = { num_of_civilian_factories_to_desert = num_of_civilian_factories }
			divide_temp_variable = {
				var = num_of_military_factories_to_desert
				value = num_of_owned_desert_states
			}
			divide_temp_variable = {
				var = num_of_civilian_factories_to_desert
				value = num_of_owned_desert_states
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { slots = num_of_military_factories_to_desert }
			add_to_temp_variable = { slots = num_of_civilian_factories_to_desert }
			every_owned_state = { limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT is_desert_state = yes }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = slots
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = num_of_military_factories_to_desert
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = num_of_civilian_factories_to_desert
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = { limit = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT is_desert_state = no } 
				remove_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 10
				}
				remove_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 10
				}
			}
		}
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.27 days = 2 }
		
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = mod_events.timed_events.59.b
	}
}
# 27 # Master of war; Doctrine research
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.60

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {

		hidden_effect = { # Immediate block shows it's effects in event desc
			random_country = {
				limit = { num_of_controlled_states > 10 }
				set_variable = { global.asteroid_country = THIS.id }
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.63 days = 8 }
				news_event = { id = mod_events.news.29 days = 2 }

					limit = { num_of_controlled_states > 10 NOT = { tag = PREV } }
					set_variable = { global.rand_country_1 = THIS.id }
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { num_of_controlled_states > 10 NOT = { OR = { tag = PREV tag = PREV.PREV } } }
						set_variable = { global.rand_country_2 = THIS.id }
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = { # So that the right option's position is random everytime
				33 = { set_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_1 }
				33 = { set_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_2 }
				33 = { set_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_3 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = asteroid_location_guessed }
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = asteroid_location_options_1

country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.63
	title = mod_events.timed_events.63.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clear_variable = global.rand_country_1
		clear_variable = global.rand_country_2
		if = { limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = asteroid_location_guessed } } 
			ROOT = { # Less manpower loss and industry evacuation
				news_event = { id = mod_events.news.30 days = 3 }
				news_event = { id = mod_events.news.32 days = 1 }
				FROM = { add_timed_idea = { idea = asteroid_prediction_correct years = 1 } }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = FROM
					modifier = cheat_opinion_modifier_good
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					ROOT = {
						launch_nuke = {
							state = PREV
							controller = ROOT
							use_nuke = no
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = { is_ai = no }
						goto_state = PREV # Moves camera to the specified state
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					} remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					} remove_building = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 2
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -10
					every_neighbor_state = {
						damage_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							damage = 1
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							damage = 1
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = infrastructure
							damage = 1
						}
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -3
						every_neighbor_state = {
							add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		} else = {
			ROOT = {
				news_event = { id = mod_events.news.32 days = 2 }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = FROM
					modifier = hostile_status
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					add_manpower = -100000
					ROOT = {
						launch_nuke = {
							state = PREV
							controller = ROOT
							use_nuke = no
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = { is_ai = no }
						goto_state = PREV # Moves camera to the specified state
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 10
					} remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 10
					} remove_building = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 5
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -10
					every_neighbor_state = {
						add_manpower = -10000
						remove_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 2
						} remove_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 2
						} remove_building = {
							type = infrastructure
							level = 2
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							damage = 2
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							damage = 2
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = infrastructure
							damage = 3
						}
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -3
						every_neighbor_state = {
							add_manpower = -1000
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 3
							}
							damage_building = {
								type = industrial_complex
								damage = 2
							}
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 3
							}
							add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

				limit = { 
					NOT = {

							value > 1
						}
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = rocket_site

						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			} else = {
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = {
							rocket_site > 1
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = rocket_site
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

# 33 # Acid rain
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.77
	title = mod_events.timed_events.77.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = mod_events.news.37 days = 2 }
			random_list = {
				10 = { 
					set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 1 }
					add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
					get_num_states_in_continent = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
						every_neighbor_state = {
							limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
							add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
						country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.78 days = 1 }

				} 10 = {

					}

					add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
					get_num_states_in_continent = yes

					random_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = australia }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
						every_neighbor_state = {
							limit = { is_on_continent = australia }
							add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
						country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.78 days = 1 }
					}
				} 10 = { 
					set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 6 }
					add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
					get_num_states_in_continent = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = north_america }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = north_america }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
						every_neighbor_state = {
							limit = { is_on_continent = north_america }
							add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
						country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.78 days = 1 }
					}
				} 10 = { 
					set_variable = { global.acid_rain_continent = 7 }
					add_to_array = { global.acid_rain_continents = global.acid_rain_continent }
					get_num_states_in_continent = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_clouds_state days = global.acid_clouds_time }
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
						every_neighbor_state = {
							limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
							add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state days = 14 }
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = { any_owned_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = acid_rain_state } } }
						country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.78 days = 1 }
					}
				} 
			}
			set_global_flag = acid_rain
			activate_mission = mod_events_acid_rain_timeout
			activate_mission = mod_events_acid_clouds_timeout
		}
	}
}

# 38 # Malta crusaders
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.87
	title = mod_events.timed_events.87.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { any_owned_state = { is_core_of = MLT } }
			release = MLT
		}
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.43 days = 2 }
		MLT = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CRU
			add_ideas = ninth_crusade
			add_war_support = 1.00
			add_stability = 1.00
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
				election_frequency = 48
				long_name = "The Ninth Crusade Order"
				name = "Crusaders"
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 1.00
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "The Leader of the Order of Malta"
				picture = GFX_portrait_CRU_crusader
				ideology = despotism
			}
			set_technology = {
				artillery1 = 1
				tech_support = 1
				tech_engineers = 1
				tech_recon = 1
				tech_maintenance_company = 1
				infantry_weapons1 = 1
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = convoy
				amount = 200
			}
			
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { OR = { state = 677 state = 344 state = 350 state = 553 state = 454 state = 799 state = 183 state = 182 state = 455 is_core_of = GRE is_core_of = TUR state = 453 state = 446 } }
			add_core_of = MLT
		}          
		every_state = {
			limit = { OR = { state = 183 state = 797 state = 182 state = 47 state = 454 state = 553 state = 799 state = 677 state = 344 state = 345 } }
			transfer_state_to = MLT
		}
		
		MLT = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Malta Knights Division"
				regiments = { 
					irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 3 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 3 y = 3 }
				}
				support = {
					recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					maintenance_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					artillery = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"The Crusaders\" division_template = \"Malta Knights Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					count = 2
					owner = MLT
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { any_owned_state = { is_core_of = MLT }  }
			MLT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					type = take_core_state
					target = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.88 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# 41 # Disease in divisions ( front line)
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.93
	title = mod_events.timed_events.93.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { any_country = { has_war = yes num_divisions > 10 } }
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_war = yes 
					num_divisions > 10
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_neighbor_of = PREV }
					PREV = {
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = PREV.PREV } }
							damage_units = {
								state = THIS
								limit = { always = no }
								org_damage = 0.5
								str_damage = 0.5
								ratio = yes
								army = yes
								navy = no
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.94 days = 1 }
			}
		} else = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes } # Probably unnecessary
				damage_units = {
					state = THIS
					limit = { always = no }
					org_damage = 0.5
					str_damage = 0.5
					ratio = yes
					army = yes
					navy = no
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.94 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

						1 = { if = { limit = { can_research = tech_signal_company4 } set_technology = { tech_signal_company4 = 1 } set_country_flag = rand_tech} }
						1 = { if = { limit = { can_research = wartime_train } set_technology = { wartime_train = 1 } set_country_flag = rand_tech} }
						1 = { if = { limit = { can_research = armored_train } set_technology = { armored_train = 1 } set_country_flag = rand_tech} }
						1 = { if = { limit = { can_research = railway_gun } set_technology = { railway_gun = 1 } set_country_flag = rand_tech} }
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = rand_tech
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.118.a
	}
}

	title = mod_events.timed_events.122.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.122.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ast_navy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.122.a
		create_equipment_variant = {
			allow_without_tech = yes
			name = "Destroyer Class"
			type = ship_hull_light_2
			role_icon_index = auto
			modules = {
				fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_battery_1
				fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_1
				fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_0
				fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
				fixed_ship_engine_slot = light_ship_engine_2
				fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_1
				mid_1_custom_slot = ship_mine_layer_1
				rear_1_custom_slot = ship_depth_charge_1
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = 20
			create_ship = {
				type = ship_hull_light_2

			}
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			allow_without_tech = yes

				type = ship_hull_submarine_2
				equipment_variant = "Submarine Class"
			}
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			allow_without_tech = yes

				fixed_ship_engine_slot = cruiser_ship_engine_2
				fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_cruiser_2
				fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = dp_ship_secondaries_1
				mid_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_1
				mid_2_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_1
				rear_1_custom_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_1
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = 3
			create_ship = {
				type = ship_hull_cruiser_2
				equipment_variant = "Cruiser Class"
			}
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			allow_without_tech = yes
			name = "Battleship Class"
			type = ship_hull_heavy_2
			role_icon_index = auto
			modules = {
				fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_heavy_battery_1
				fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
				fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_1
				fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
				fixed_ship_engine_slot = heavy_ship_engine_1
				fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = dp_ship_secondaries_1
				fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_bb_1
				front_1_custom_slot = ship_heavy_battery_1
				mid_1_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_2
				mid_2_custom_slot = dp_ship_secondaries_1

		}
		create_ship = {
			type = ship_hull_heavy_2
			equipment_variant = "Battleship Class"
		}create_ship = {
			type = ship_hull_heavy_2
			equipment_variant = "Battleship Class"
		}

			allow_without_tech = yes
			name = "Carrier Class"
			type = ship_hull_carrier_2

# 57 # Radars

	}

country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.124
	title = mod_events.timed_events.124.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.124.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_radar_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.124.a
		set_technology = {
			decimetric_radar = 1
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					has_built = {
						type = radar_station
						value > 1
					}
				}
			}
			capital_scope = { # The first time is going to be at the capital
				add_building_construction = {
					type = radar_station
					level = 6
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		} else = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = {
						radar_station > 1
					} 
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = radar_station
					level = 6
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

	title = mod_events.timed_events.132.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.132.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_mils_to_civs
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = mod_events.timed_events.132.a
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { check_variable = { arms_factory_level > 1 } }
			set_temp_variable = { 
				var = mils_to_convert
				value = arms_factory_level
				tooltip = mils_in_state
			}
			divide_temp_variable = { mils_to_convert = 2 }
			round_temp_variable = mils_to_convert
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = mils_to_convert
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = mils_to_convert
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}
# 62 # Allies backstab
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.133
	title = mod_events.timed_events.133.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { any_country = { is_subject = no is_in_faction_with = ENG is_major = no } }
			random_country = {
				limit = { is_subject = no is_in_faction_with = ENG is_major = no }
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.134 }
			}
		} else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes num_faction_members > 1 }
				random_country = {
					limit = { is_subject = no is_in_faction_with = PREV }
					country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.135 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.134
	title = mod_events.timed_events.134.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.134.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.134.a
		ENG = {
			remove_from_faction = ROOT
			declare_war_on = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			THIS = {
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			target = ended_puppet
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_subject_of = ROOT }

				chance = 50
				overlord = { end_puppet = PREV }
				declare_war_on = {
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					target = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = events_tooltip_1
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.137.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.57 days = 2 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.142
	title = mod_events.timed_events.142.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = { OR = { is_major = yes is_ai = no } }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.143 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.144
	title = mod_events.timed_events.144.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = { OR = { is_major = yes is_ai = no } }
			set_variable = { global.generalissimo_country = THIS.id }
			random_army_leader = {
				unit_leader_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.145 }
				set_variable = { global.generalissimo = THIS.id }
			}
		}
	}
}

# 68 # ZIN
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.146
	title = mod_events.timed_events.146.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes


	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			limit = { is_capital = no }
			owner = {
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.147 }
			}
			transfer_state_to = ZIN
			add_core_of = ZIN
			ZIN = { load_oob = "ZIN_1936" }
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Guardians of ZIN\" division_template = \"Guardians of ZIN\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
				count = 6
				owner = ZIN
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Cavalry of ZIN\" division_template = \"Cavalry of ZIN\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
				count = 3
				owner = ZIN
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.147
	title = mod_events.timed_events.147.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.147.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_zin
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.147.a
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.60 days = 1 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.147.b
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.60 days = 1 }
		create_wargoal = {
			target = ZIN
			type = annex_everything
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.148
	title = mod_events.timed_events.148.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.148.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_zin
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.148.a
		remove_ideas = punishment_from_gods
		white_peace = {
			tag = ZIN
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ZIN } } # Checks core territory
			capital_scope = {
				transfer_state_to = ZIN
				add_core_of = ZIN
			}
		} else = {
			ZIN = {
				every_core_state = {
					every_neighbor_state = {
						limit = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						transfer_state_to = ZIN
						add_core_of = ZIN
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				any_country = { NOT = { tag = ZIN } has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_stability < 0.5
				has_war_support < 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_stability < 0.25
				has_war_support < 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_stability < 0.10
				has_war_support < 0.10
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_manpower < 10000
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_damaged_buildings = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				all_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						non_damaged_building_level = {
							building = arms_factory
							level < 2
						}
						non_damaged_building_level = {
							building = industrial_complex
							level < 2
						}
						non_damaged_building_level = {
							building = infrastructure
							level < 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.148.b
		add_political_power = -10
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
}

	title = mod_events.timed_events.150.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.150.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.150.a
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.61 days = 3 }
		add_war_support = 0.25
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { any_owned_state = { is_core_of = CHI } NOT = { any_core_state = { is_core_of = CHI } } }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.151 }
		}

# 77 # Free equipment from major to minor
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.173
	title = mod_events.timed_events.173.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { is_major = yes is_ai = no }
				OR = {
					# Infantry
					has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 1000 }
					has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 150 }
					has_equipment = { anti_air_equipment > 100 }
					has_equipment = { anti_tank_equipment > 100 }
					has_equipment = { support_equipment > 200 }
					# Motorized/Supply
					has_equipment = { motorized_equipment > 100 }
					has_equipment = { armored_car_equipment > 100 }
					has_equipment = { mechanized_equipment > 100 }
					has_equipment = { amphibious_mechanized_equipment > 100 }
					has_equipment = { train_equipment > 10 }
					has_equipment = { convoy > 100 }
					# Planes
					has_equipment = { small_plane_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { cv_small_plane_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { small_plane_cas_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { cv_small_plane_cas_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { cv_small_plane_naval_bomber_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { small_plane_suicide_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { cv_small_plane_suicide_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { jet_fighter_equipment > 50 }
					has_equipment = { rocket_interceptor_equipment > 50 }
					has_equipment = { medium_plane_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { medium_plane_fighter_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { medium_plane_scout_plane_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { jet_tac_bomber_equipment > 50 }
					has_equipment = { large_plane_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { large_plane_maritime_patrol_plane_airframe > 50 }
					has_equipment = { jet_strat_bomber_equipment > 50 }
					has_equipment = { transport_plane_equipment > 50 }
					# Tanks
					has_equipment = { light_tank_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { light_tank_aa_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { light_tank_artillery_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { light_tank_destroyer_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { light_tank_amphibious_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { light_tank_flame_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { medium_tank_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { medium_tank_aa_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { medium_tank_artillery_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { medium_tank_destroyer_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { medium_tank_amphibious_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { medium_tank_flame_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { heavy_tank_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { heavy_tank_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { heavy_tank_aa_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { heavy_tank_artillery_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { heavy_tank_destroyer_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { heavy_tank_amphibious_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { heavy_tank_flame_chassis > 100 }
					# Late game
					has_equipment = { modern_tank_chassis > 50 }
					has_equipment = { super_heavy_tank_chassis > 50 }
					has_equipment = { amphibious_tank_chassis > 100 }
					has_equipment = { railway_gun_equipment > 1 }
				}
			}
			# Get random minors
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_major = no NOT = { is_ally_with = PREV } is_in_faction = no is_subject = no }
				set_variable = { global.random_minor_1 = THIS.id }
				random_other_country = {
					limit = { is_major = no NOT = { is_ally_with = PREV.PREV } is_in_faction = no is_subject = no }
					set_variable = { global.random_minor_2 = THIS.id }
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { is_major = no NOT = { is_ally_with = PREV.PREV.PREV tag = PREV.PREV } is_in_faction = no is_subject = no }
						set_variable = { global.random_minor_3 = THIS.id }
					}
				}
			}
			
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.174 }
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {

				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.243 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.243
	title = mod_events.timed_events.176.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.176.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_mongolia_fortify_border
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
				set_variable = { global.border_war_country = PREV.id }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.176.a
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_political_power = 50
		var:global.border_war_country = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.177 days = 5 } }
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.78 days = 2 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.176.b
		add_war_support = -0.20
		add_political_power = -100
		declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = global.border_war_country
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.177
	title = mod_events.timed_events.177.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.177.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_mongolia_fortify_border
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.177.a
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = FROM } }
			FROM = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } }
					FROM = {
						start_border_war = {
							change_state_after_war = yes
							attacker = {
								state = PREV.PREV.PREV
								num_provinces = 100 # just to make sure all the provinces are used
								on_win = mod_events.timed_events.178
								on_lose = mod_events.timed_events.179
								on_cancel = mod_events.timed_events.180
							}	
							defender = {
								state = PREV
								num_provinces = 100
								on_win = mod_events.timed_events.178
								on_lose = mod_events.timed_events.179
								on_cancel = mod_events.timed_events.180
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 79 # The Master
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.181
	title = mod_events.timed_events.181.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.181.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_indonesia_handover
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = fight_for_minor
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { is_major = no num_of_factories < ROOT.num_of_factories has_war = no is_in_faction = no }
				set_variable = { global.minor_to_attract = THIS.id }
				ROOT = { give_guarantee = PREV }
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_enemy_ideology = yes OR = { is_major = yes num_of_factories > ROOT.num_of_factories } }
					set_country_flag = fight_for_minor
					give_guarantee = PREV
				}
			}
			every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = fight_for_minor } add_to_array = { global.masters_array = THIS.id } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.181.a
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.182
	title = mod_events.timed_events.182.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.182.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hitler_handshake
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mod_events.timed_events.182.a
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_guaranteed = var:global.minor_to_attract }
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = [MINOR_TO_ATTRACT]
						relation = guarantee
						active = no
					}
				}
				MINOR_TO_ATTRACT = "[?global.minor_to_attract.GetID]"
			}
		}
		puppet = {
			target = var:global.minor_to_attract
			end_wars = yes
		}
		news_event = { id = mod_events.news.66 days = 1 }
	}
	
}

# 89 # Tech sharing groups
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.207
	title = mod_events.timed_events.207.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { OR = { tag = ENG tag = SOV tag = GER tag = JAP tag = USA } }
			
			if = { limit = { tag = ENG }
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research
			} else_if = { limit = { tag = SOV } 
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = comintern_research
			}else_if = { limit = { tag = GER } 
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = axis_research
			}else_if = { limit = { tag = JAP } 
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = japanese_research
			}else_if = { limit = { tag = USA } 
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = us_research
			}
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.209 }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { NOT = { OR = { tag = ENG tag = SOV tag = GER tag = JAP tag = USA } } }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.208 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.208
	title = mod_events.timed_events.208.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.208.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_research_lab
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research
		ENG = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.210 } }
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ENG
			modifier = small_increase
		}
		name = mod_events.timed_events.208.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5 
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = { 
					has_government = ENG
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = ENG
		}
	}
	option = {
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = comintern_research
		SOV = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.210 } }
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SOV
			modifier = small_increase
		}
		name = mod_events.timed_events.208.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5 
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_government = SOV
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = SOV
		}
	}
	option = {
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = axis_research
		GER = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.210 } }
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = small_increase
		}

			factor = 5

			}

			target = JAP
			modifier = small_increase
		}

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5 
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_government = JAP
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = JAP
			ROOT = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = us_research
		USA = { country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.210 } }
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = small_increase
		}
		name = mod_events.timed_events.208.f

				}
				OR = { 
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = USA
		}
	}
	option = {

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		
	}

# 91 # The Great revolution
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.213
	title = mod_events.timed_events.213.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	
	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { REV.temp_oob_container = owner.id }
			transfer_state_to = REV
		}
		REV = { load_oob = "REV_1936" create_faction = revolution_front } # if country doesn't exist, does nothing
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_owned_by = REV }
			transfer_state_to = REV.temp_oob_container
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = SOV }
			add_claim_by = REV
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.214 }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_government = communism }
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.215 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.214
	title = mod_events.timed_events.214.t
	desc = mod_events.timed_events.214.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_lenin
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { rand_communist_states = party_popularity@communism }
			multiply_temp_variable = { rand_communist_states = num_owned_states }
			round_temp_variable = rand_communist_states
			if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { rand_communist_states = 0 } } }
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = { impassable = no }
							random_select_amount = [COMMUNIST_STATES_AMOUNT] # doesn't allow normal variable input
							transfer_state_to = REV
							add_core_of = REV
							if = { limit = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Revolutinaries of Arabia\" division_template = \"Regular Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
									owner = REV
									count = 1
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Believers of the Cause\" division_template = \"Red Army Irregulars\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
									owner = REV
									count = 2
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Red Camels\" division_template = \"Red Army Cavalry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
									owner = REV
									count = 1
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
							} else_if = { limit = { is_on_continent = asia }
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Revolutionaries\" division_template = \"Regular Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
									owner = REV
									count = 1
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Belivers of the Cause\" division_template = \"Red Army Irregulars\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
									owner = REV
									count = 1
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Red Cossacks\" division_template = \"Red Army Cavalry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
									owner = REV
									count = 2
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
							} else_if = { limit = { is_on_continent = south_america } 
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Revolucionarios\" division_template = \"Regular Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
									owner = REV
									count = 2
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Creyentes de la Causa\" division_template = \"Red Army Irregulars\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
									owner = REV
									count = 1
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Cosacos Rojos\" division_template = \"Red Army Cavalry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
									owner = REV
									count = 1
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
							} else = {
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Revolutionaries\" division_template = \"Regular Revolutionary Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
									owner = REV
									count = 2
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"The Red Army\" division_template = \"Red Army Infantry\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
									owner = REV
									count = 2
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Guards of Lenin\" division_template = \"Lenin's Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
									owner = REV
									count = 1
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Red Cossacks\" division_template = \"Red Army Cavalry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
									owner = REV
									count = 1
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
					COMMUNIST_STATES_AMOUNT = "[?rand_communist_states|.0]"
				}
				
			}
			REV = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 50
		name = mod_events.timed_events.214.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

# 95 # Occupation revolt
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.225
	title = mod_events.timed_events.225.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = { is_government_in_exile = yes }
			random_enemy_country = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
				}
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Revolt Division"
				regiments = { 
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					cavalry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					cavalry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Rebels\" division_template = \"Revolt Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = PREV
					count = 1
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.226 }
		}
	}
}

# 98 # New ore
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.231
	title = mod_events.timed_events.231.t

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = special_ore_state } } }
			set_variable = { ore_state = THIS.id }
			set_variable = { global.ore_state_container = THIS.id }
			ROOT = { goto_state = PREV }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = special_ore_state } # just to indicate where the special state is
			owner = { 
				country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.232 }
				add_ideas = special_iron_ore
			}
		}
	}
}

# 99 # Desert storm
country_event = {
	id = mod_events.timed_events.233
	title = mod_events.timed_events.233.t
	
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 1 }
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = europe }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
					}
				}10 = {
					set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 2 }
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
					}
				}10 = {
					set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 3 }
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = asia }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
					}
				}10 = {
					set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 4 }
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = africa }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
					}
				}10 = {
					set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 5 }
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = australia }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
					}
				}10 = {
					set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 6 }
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = north_america }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
					}
				}10 = {
					set_variable = { global.desert_storm_continent = 7 }
					every_state = {
						limit = { is_on_continent = south_america }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = desert_storm days = 180 }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = mod_events.timed_events.236 }
		}
	}
		
}
